Source Code

These source-code files derive from a printout of Luminary 116 (the Apollo 12 Lunar Module guidance computer program), from the personal library of original AGC developer Don Eyles, digitally photographed at archive.org, financially sponsored by Ron Burkey, and transcribed to source code by a team of volunteers. This colorized, syntax-highlighted form was created by assembling that transcribed source code. Note that the full page images are available on the Virtual AGC project page at archive.org, while reduced-size images are presented at the VirtualAGC project website. Report or fix any transcription errors at the Virtual AGC project code repository.

Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 116 OF AGC PROGRAM LUMINARY BY NASA 2021112-071
	19:09 AUG. 11,1969
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision. 

021114,000002:                                                                                                  ## Copyright:   Public domain.

021121,000009:                                                                                                  ##              requirements of the yaYUL assembler rather than the

021130,000018:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-13 RSB  Proofed comment text via 3-way diff vs
021131,000019:                                                                                                  ##                              Luminary 99 and 131.
021132,000020:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-16 RSB  Comment-text fixes identified in 5-way
021133,000021:                                                                                                  ##                              side-by-side diff of Luminary 69/99/116/131/210.
021134,000022:                                                                                                  ##              2017-03-19 HG   Fix operator CALL  --> VLOAD

021136,000024:                                                                                                  ##                              Fix operand   ENDRRD29 --> ENDR29RD

021140,000028:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021141,000029:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021142,000030:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021143,000031:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021144,000032:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021145,000033: 
021146,000034:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021147,000035:                                                                                                  #  STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER
021148,000036:                                                                                                  #  THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021149,000037:                                                                                                  #  ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021150,000038:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021151,000039: 
021152,000040:                                                                                                  #  ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021153,000041:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021154,000042:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)               FLAGUP
021155,000043:                                                                                                  #    GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                FLAGDOWN
021156,000044:                                                                                                  #    R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)             BANKCALL
021157,000045:                                                                                                  #    LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)              TASKOVER
021158,000046:                                                                                                  #    LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021159,000047:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021160,000048:                                                                                                  #    R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                   ENDOFJOB
021161,000049:                                                                                                  #    R22LEM  (DATA READ)                      GOPERF1
021162,000050:                                                                                                  #    R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)
021163,000051:                                                                                                  #    PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021164,000052:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021165,000053:                                                                                                  #    P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021166,000054:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021167,000055:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021168,000056:                                                                                                  #    RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021169,000057:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021170,000058:                                                                                                  #    TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021171,000059:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021172,000060:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021173,000061:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,RNDVZFLG,ACMODFLG,VEHUPFLG,UPDATFLG,TRACKFLG,
021174,000062:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021175,000063:                                                                                                  #    CENTRALS-A,Q,L
021176,000064: 25,2073  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021177,000065: 
021178,000066: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
021179,000067: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
021180,000068: 24,2000                                           BANK                                           
021181,000069: 
021182,000070: 24,2000  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021183,000071: 24,2000                                           COUNT*   $$/P20

021612,000500:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021613,000501:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021614,000502:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 3
021615,000503:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
021616,000504:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021617,000505: 
021618,000506:                                                                                                  #    THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021619,000507:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021620,000508:                                                                                                  #  CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021621,000509:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021622,000510:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021623,000511:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021624,000512:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021625,000513:                                                                                                  #    BANKCALL                      FLAGUP
021626,000514:                                                                                                  #    R02BOTH  (IMU STATUS CHECK)   ENDOFJOB
021627,000515:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM   (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)  WAITLIST
021628,000516:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER                      FINDVAC
021629,000517:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES  -
021630,000518:                                                                                                  #    P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS-ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021631,000519:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM(P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021632,000520:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021633,000521:                                                                                                  #    NONE
021634,000522:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021635,000523:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

021638,000526:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS

021684,000572:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021685,000573:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021686,000574:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021687,000575:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
021688,000576:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021689,000577: 
021690,000578:                                                                                                  #    TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021691,000579:                                                                                                  #  LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021692,000580:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021693,000581:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
021694,000582:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R22LEM
021695,000583:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021696,000584:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.1           GOFLASH        WAITLIST
021697,000585:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.2           PRIOLARM       BANKCALL
021698,000586:                                                                                                  #    LSR22.3           R61LEM
021699,000587:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
021700,000588:                                                                                                  #    R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE,UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021701,000589:                                                                                                  #  UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021702,000590:                                                                                                  #  R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021703,000591:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021704,000592:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM
021705,000593:                                                                                                  #  PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021706,000594:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021707,000595:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR22.3
021708,000596:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021709,000597:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3
021710,000598:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021711,000599:                                                                                                  #    NOANGFLG
021712,000600:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021713,000601:                                                                                                  #    SEE LSR22.1,LSR22.2,LSR22.3

021890,000778:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021891,000779:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021892,000780:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
021893,000781:                                                                                                  #  BY P VOLANTE
021894,000782:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021895,000783: 
021896,000784:                                                                                                  #    TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021897,000785:                                                                                                  #  OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR. ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021898,000786:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021899,000787:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
021900,000788:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R21LEM
021901,000789:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021902,000790:                                                                                                  #    FINDVAC        FLAGUP           ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021903,000791:                                                                                                  #    NOVAC          INTPRET          LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021904,000792:                                                                                                  #    WAITLIST       JOBSLEEP         JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021905,000793:                                                                                                  #    TASKOVER       BANKCALL         RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021906,000794:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021907,000795:                                                                                                  #    WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED,BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021908,000796:                                                                                                  #  WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER(BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021909,000797:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
021910,000798:                                                                                                  #    PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021911,000799:                                                                                                  #  THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021912,000800:                                                                                                  #  ACQUISITION
021913,000801:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021914,000802:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
021915,000803:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021916,000804:                                                                                                  #    RRTARGET,RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021917,000805:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021918,000806:                                                                                                  #    LOSCMFLG      LOKONSW
021919,000807:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021920,000808:                                                                                                  #    SEE LPS20.1,RRDESSM
021921,000809: 24,2675  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021922,000810: 24,2675                                           COUNT*   $$/R21

021924,000812: 24,2676           00006                           EXTEND

022095,000983:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM

022100,000988: 
022101,000989:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022102,000990:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -

022108,000996:                                                                                                  #    IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1 ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23

022166,001054:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022167,001055:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022168,001056:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO - 2
022169,001057:                                                                                                  #  BY  P. VOLANTE
022170,001058:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022171,001059: 
022172,001060:                                                                                                  #    TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022173,001061:                                                                                                  #  FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022174,001062:                                                                                                  #  THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
022175,001063:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022176,001064:                                                                                                  #           CAF    PRIONN
022177,001065:                                                                                                  #           TC     FINDVAC
022178,001066:                                                                                                  #           EBANK= DATAGOOD
022179,001067:                                                                                                  #           2CADR  R24LEM
022180,001068:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022181,001069:                                                                                                  #    FLAGUP        FLAGDOWN      BANKCALL
022182,001070:                                                                                                  #    R61LEM        GOFLASHR      FINDVAC
022183,001071:                                                                                                  #    ENDOFJOB      NOVAC         LSR24.1
022184,001072:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022185,001073:                                                                                                  #    ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.HE CAN EITHER
022186,001074:                                                                                                  #  REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022187,001075:                                                                                                  #  PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022188,001076:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022189,001077:                                                                                                  #    SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022190,001078:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022191,001079:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022192,001080:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022193,001081:                                                                                                  #    SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022194,001082:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022195,001083:                                                                                                  #    SRCHOPT,ACMODFLG
022196,001084: 24,3207  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022197,001085: 24,3207                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
022198,001086: 24,3207           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
022199,001087: 24,3210           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
022200,001088: 24,3211           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
022201,001089: 24,3212           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022202,001090: 24,3213           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022203,001091: 24,3214           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022204,001092: 24,3215           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022205,001093: 24,3216           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

022268,001156:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
022269,001157:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022270,001158:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO : 3                      DATE: 4-11-67
022271,001159:                                                                                                  #  MOD BY : P VOLANTE  SDC
022272,001160: 
022273,001161: 
022274,001162:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION-
022275,001163:                                                                                                  #    TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
022276,001164:                                                                                                  #  TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
022277,001165:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE.
022278,001166:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE-
022279,001167:                                                                                                  #           TC     BANKCALL
022280,001168:                                                                                                  #           CADR   R61LEM
022281,001169:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022282,001170:                                                                                                  #      LPS20.1       VECPOINT
022283,001171:                                                                                                  #      KALCMAN3
022284,001172: 
022285,001173: 
022286,001174:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES-
022287,001175:                                                                                                  #    NORMAL RETURN IS TO CALLER + 1
022288,001176:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES-
022289,001177:                                                                                                  #    TERMINATE P20 + R61 BY BRANCHING TO P20END IF BOTH TRACKFLAG +
022290,001178:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS FLAG ARE NOT SET.
022291,001179:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
022292,001180:                                                                                                  #    SEE OUTPUT FOR LPS20.1 + ATTITUDE MANEUVER ROUTINE (R60)
022293,001181:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022294,001182:                                                                                                  #    GENRET USED TO SAVE Q FOR RETURN
022295,001183:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022296,001184:                                                                                                  #    3AXISFLG
022297,001185:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
022298,001186:                                                                                                  #    SEE SUBROUTINES
022299,001187: 23,2000                                           SETLOC   R61                                   
022300,001188: 23,2000                                           BANK                                           
022301,001189: 23,2116  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022302,001190: 23,2116                                           COUNT*   $$/R61                                
022303,001191: 23,2116           04645        R61LEM             TC       MAKECADR                              
022304,001192: 23,2117           55142                           TS       GENRET                                
022305,001193: 23,2120           05504                           TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET R61 FLAG
022306,001194: 23,2121           00024                           ADRES    R61FLAG                               
022307,001195: 23,2122           02152                           TC       R61C+L02                              
022308,001196: 23,2123           04645        R65LEM             TC       MAKECADR

022482,001370:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRLIMCHK                                                  ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022483,001371: 
022484,001372:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022485,001373:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022486,001374:                                                                                                  #  THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE. INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022487,001375:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2. THE CURRENT RR
022488,001376:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022489,001377:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022490,001378:                                                                                                  #  MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022491,001379:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022492,001380:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022493,001381:                                                                                                  #  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022494,001382:                                                                                                  #  MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022495,001383:                                                                                                  #  BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF WITHIN
022496,001384:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022497,001385:                                                                                                  #  AND -125 (+235) DEGREES. IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2. IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022498,001386:                                                                                                  #  TO L +3.
022499,001387: 
022500,001388:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022501,001389:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022502,001390:                                                                                                  #  L +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022503,001391: 
022504,001392:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022505,001393:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022506,001394:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022507,001395:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT EBANK).
022508,001396: 
022509,001397:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  MAGSUB
022510,001398:

022512,001400:

022514,001402: 
022515,001403:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L + 2 (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022516,001404:                                                                                                  #  L + 3 (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)

022562,001450:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  SETTRKF                                                  . IF EITHER:
022563,001451: 
022564,001452:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022565,001453:                                                                                                  #  SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022566,001454:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022567,001455:                                                                                                  #  IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022568,001456:                                                                                                  #  IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022569,001457:                                                                                                  #  1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022570,001458:                                                                                                  #  AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022571,001459:                                                                                                  #  2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022572,001460:                                                                                                  #  8,5)
022573,001461:                                                                                                  #  3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022574,001462:                                                                                                  #  THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022575,001463:                                                                                                  #  IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022576,001464:                                                                                                  #  LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022577,001465:                                                                                                  #  THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022578,001466:                                                                                                  #  TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022579,001467:                                                                                                  #  A ) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022580,001468:                                                                                                  #  B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022581,001469:                                                                                                  #  EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022582,001470:                                                                                                  #  C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022583,001471:                                                                                                  #  WITH EITHER THE AL
022584,001472: 
022585,001473:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022586,001474:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  SETTRKF
022587,001475: 
022588,001476:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED: IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022589,001477:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022590,001478: 
022591,001479:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022592,001480: 
022593,001481:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022633,001521:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022634,001522: 
022635,001523:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022636,001524: 
022637,001525:                                                                                                  #  RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022638,001526:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022639,001527:                                                                                                  #  INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022640,001528:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE. UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022641,001529:                                                                                                  #  WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022642,001530:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022643,001531:                                                                                                  #  INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501. A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022644,001532:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7). IF
022645,001533:                                                                                                  #  SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022646,001534:                                                                                                  #  FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022647,001535:                                                                                                  #  RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM. IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022648,001536:                                                                                                  #  TO TASKOVER.
022649,001537: 
022650,001538:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022651,001539:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING
022652,001540:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022653,001541: 
022654,001542:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022655,001543:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, STATE
022656,001544: 
022657,001545:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022658,001546: 
022659,001547:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022660,001548:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022661,001549: 
022662,001550:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022663,001551: 
022664,001552:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_   TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022665,001553: 
022666,001554: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022667,001555: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022668,001556: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022669,001557:

022681,001569:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022682,001570: 
022683,001571:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022684,001572:                                                                                                  #  RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022685,001573:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022686,001574:                                                                                                  #  LAMP IF REQUIRED. INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022687,001575:                                                                                                  #  BIT 1) IS SET. FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022688,001576:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER
022689,001577:                                                                                                  #  WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022690,001578:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022691,001579:                                                                                                  #  TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES. THE
022692,001580:                                                                                                  #  RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED. THE
022693,001581:                                                                                                  #  CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022694,001582:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES. IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022695,001583:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022696,001584:                                                                                                  #  IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022697,001585:                                                                                                  #  INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1. SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022698,001586:                                                                                                  #  SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022699,001587: 
022700,001588:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L  TC  RRZEROSB (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022701,001589:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022702,001590:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022703,001591: 
022704,001592:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022705,001593: 
022706,001594:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022707,001595:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022708,001596: 
022709,001597:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022710,001598: 
022711,001599:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)
022712,001600: 
022713,001601: 25,2102           00006        RRZEROSB           EXTEND                                         
022714,001602: 25,2103           23312                           QXCH     RRRET                                 
022715,001603: 25,2104           34753                           CAF      BIT1                                  #  BIT 13 OF RADMODES MUST BE SET BEFORE
022716,001604: 25,2105           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.
022717,001605: 25,2106           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                #  TURN ON ZERO RR CDU
022718,001606: 25,2107           05221                           TC       FIXDELAY                              
022719,001607: 25,2110           00002                           DEC      2          B-14                       
022720,001608:

022755,001643:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022756,001644:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022757,001645:                                                                                                  #  DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022758,001646:                                                                                                  #  TO A SAFE POSITION. INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022759,001647:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022760,001648:                                                                                                  #  AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022761,001649:                                                                                                  #  DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS. THE RR
022762,001650:                                                                                                  #  TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022763,001651:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING. IN EITHER
022764,001652:                                                                                                  #  CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022765,001653:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12). RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022766,001654:                                                                                                  #  TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022767,001655:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022768,001656:                                                                                                  #  MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED. RRSONLY IS THEN
022769,001657:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022770,001658:                                                                                                  #  -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022771,001659:                                                                                                  #  REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022772,001660:                                                                                                  #  FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022773,001661:                                                                                                  #  REPOSRPT. HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS
022774,001662:                                                                                                  #  REMOVED. A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022775,001663:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10). IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES. IF NOT PRESENT
022776,001664:                                                                                                  #  INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022777,001665:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022778,001666:                                                                                                  #  TASKOVER.
022779,001667: 
022780,001668:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022781,001669:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022782,001670:                                                                                                  #  NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022783,001671: 
022784,001672:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022785,001673:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
022786,001674: 
022787,001675:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022788,001676:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022789,001677: 
022790,001678:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022791,001679:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022792,001680: 
022793,001681:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022794,001682: 
022795,001683:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES
022796,001684: 
022797,001685: 25,2140           02167        DORREPOS           TC       SETRRECR                              #  SET UP RR CDU ERROR COUNTERS.
022798,001686: 
022799,001687:                                                                                                  #  ALARM 501 DELETED IN DANCE 279 PER PCR 97.

022844,001732:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                 IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022845,001733: 
022846,001734:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                               S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022847,001735:                                                                                                  #  REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE. IT DRIVES THE
022848,001736:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022849,001737:                                                                                                  #  180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022850,001738:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022851,001739:                                                                                                  #  TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022852,001740:                                                                                                  #  INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL. ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022853,001741:                                                                                                  #  AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS). INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022854,001742:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED. CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022855,001743:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022856,001744:                                                                                                  #  OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2. RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022857,001745:                                                                                                  #  THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022858,001746:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN. CONTROL IS AGAIN
022859,001747:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022860,001748:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022861,001749:                                                                                                  #  -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1. RMODINV
022862,001750:                                                                                                  #  IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022863,001751:                                                                                                  #  RR ANTENNA MODE. THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022864,001752:                                                                                                  #  IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE. THE PROGRAM
022865,001753:                                                                                                  #  THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022866,001754: 
022867,001755:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022868,001756:                                                                                                  #  FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022869,001757:                                                                                                  #  THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022870,001758:                                                                                                  #  DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022871,001759:                                                                                                  #  OTHER MODE.
022872,001760: 
022873,001761:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022874,001762:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES
022875,001763: 
022876,001764:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022877,001765:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY, RRSONLY, RMODINV (ACTUALLY PART OF)
022878,001766:

022880,001768:                                                                                                  #  NONE

022938,001826:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_  RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022939,001827: 
022940,001828:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022941,001829:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022942,001830:                                                                                                  #  RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION. IT DRIVES TO
022943,001831:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN 1 DEGREE. INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022944,001832:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED. IF BOTH EXIST,
022945,001833:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS). THIS INDICATES
022946,001834:                                                                                                  #  THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022947,001835:                                                                                                  #  WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022948,001836:                                                                                                  #  REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11). IF NONE
022949,001837:                                                                                                  #  OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022950,001838:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE. IF YES,
022951,001839:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE. IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022952,001840:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022953,001841:                                                                                                  #  ANGLE SET = 0. FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022954,001842:                                                                                                  #  REPEATED.
022955,001843: 
022956,001844:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE: L-1 CAF *ANGLE*  (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022957,001845:                                                                                                  #  L  TC  RRTONLY (TRUNNION ONLY)
022958,001846:                                                                                                  #  RRSONLY (SHAFT ONLY)
022959,001847:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022960,001848:                                                                                                  #  RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022961,001849: 
022962,001850:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022963,001851:                                                                                                  #  C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022964,001852:

022966,001854:                                                                                                  #  FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
022967,001855: 
022968,001856:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022969,001857:                                                                                                  #  NONE
022970,001858:

022974,001862:                                                                                                  #  BITS 14, 11)

023026,001914:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
023027,001915: 
023028,001916:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023029,001917:                                                                                                  #  RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023030,001918:                                                                                                  #  ERROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023031,001919:                                                                                                  #  GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023032,001920:                                                                                                  #  TO THE DESIRED VALUES. INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023033,001921:                                                                                                  #  THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023034,001922:                                                                                                  #  384 PULSES. IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023035,001923:                                                                                                  #  LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES. THE DIFFERENCE IS
023036,001924:                                                                                                  #  THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
023037,001925:                                                                                                  #  THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023038,001926:                                                                                                  #  THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023039,001927:                                                                                                  #  PASS). FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023040,001928:                                                                                                  #  OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023041,001929:                                                                                                  #  ARE SET. THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023042,001930: 
023043,001931:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:

023131,002019:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
023132,002020: 
023133,002021:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023134,002022:                                                                                                  #  THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023135,002023:                                                                                                  #  WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023136,002024:                                                                                                  #  (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023137,002025:                                                                                                  #  ORIENTATION. INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023138,002026:                                                                                                  #  TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023139,002027:                                                                                                  #  MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
023140,002028:                                                                                                  #  RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023141,002029:                                                                                                  #  TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023142,002030:                                                                                                  #  RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023143,002031:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
023144,002032:                                                                                                  #  LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023145,002033:                                                                                                  #  REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES. IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
023146,002034:                                                                                                  #  CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED. FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023147,002035:                                                                                                  #  ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023148,002036:                                                                                                  #  TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023149,002037:                                                                                                  #  LIMITS. IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023150,002038:                                                                                                  #  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023151,002039:                                                                                                  #  INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023152,002040:                                                                                                  #  EXITING TO STARTDES. IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023153,002041:                                                                                                  #  OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023154,002042:                                                                                                  #  BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023155,002043:                                                                                                  #  TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023156,002044: 
023157,002045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023158,002046:                                                                                                  #  L  STCALL  RRTARGET  (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023159,002047:                                                                                                  #  L+1  RRDESSM
023160,002048:                                                                                                  #  L+2  BASIC  (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023161,002049:                                                                                                  #  L+3  BASIC  (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023162,002050: 
023163,002051:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023164,002052:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET, RADMODES
023165,002053: 
023166,002054:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023167,002055:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023168,002056:                                                                                                  #  PART OF), RMODINV
023169,002057: 
023170,002058:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023171,002059:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023172,002060:
