023218,002106:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                 STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
023219,002107: 
023220,002108:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                 CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
023221,002109:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
023222,002110:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023223,002111:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
023224,002112:                                                                                                  #  OPERATION. IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023225,002113:                                                                                                  #  ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023226,002114:                                                                                                  #  OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023227,002115:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATION BEGINS. INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023228,002116:                                                                                                  #  THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023229,002117:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5). BIT 10
023230,002118:                                                                                                  #  OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023231,002119:                                                                                                  #  THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF SET,
023232,002120:                                                                                                  #  THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023233,002121:                                                                                                  #  AND RRDESNB). THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023234,002122:                                                                                                  #  ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023235,002123:                                                                                                  #  REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023236,002124:                                                                                                  #  WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023237,002125:                                                                                                  #  AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023238,002126:                                                                                                  #  DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023239,002127:                                                                                                  #  COUNTERS. A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023240,002128:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023241,002129: 
023242,002130:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023243,002131:                                                                                                  #  FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023244,002132: 
023245,002133:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023246,002134:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023247,002135: 
023248,002136:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023249,002137:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR, WAITLIST
023250,002138: 
023251,002139:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_

023390,002278:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023391,002279: 
023392,002280:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023393,002281:                                                                                                  #  BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023394,002282:                                                                                                  #  ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION. INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023395,002283:                                                                                                  #  REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS. IF SO,
023396,002284:                                                                                                  #  CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023397,002285:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023398,002286:                                                                                                  #  FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED. IF
023399,002287:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023400,002288:                                                                                                  #  AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND. IF THE REPOSITION
023401,002289:                                                                                                  #  FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023402,002290:                                                                                                  #  BIT 15) IS CHECKED. IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023403,002291:                                                                                                  #  MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023404,002292:                                                                                                  #  REPEATING AT STDESIG. IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023405,002293:                                                                                                  #  TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023406,002294:                                                                                                  #  IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023407,002295:                                                                                                  #  BIT 10) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023408,002296:                                                                                                  #  CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM. IF DESIGNATE
023409,002297:                                                                                                  #  IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023410,002298:                                                                                                  #  EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023411,002299:                                                                                                  #  SIGNAL. IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023412,002300:                                                                                                  #  RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023413,002301:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023414,002302:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND. IF
023415,002303:                                                                                                  #  TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023416,002304:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023417,002305:                                                                                                  #  BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023418,002306: 
023419,002307:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023420,002308:                                                                                                  #  WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023421,002309:                                                                                                  #  TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023422,002310:                                                                                                  #  TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023423,002311: 
023424,002312:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023425,002313:                                                                                                  #  DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023426,002314: 
023427,002315:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023428,002316:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023429,002317: 
023430,002318:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023431,002319: 
023432,002320:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023433,002321:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023434,002322: 
023435,002323:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023436,002324:                                                                                                  #  ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023437,002325:                                                                                                  #  RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023438,002326: 
023439,002327: 25,2604           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES                              
023440,002328:

Page 548

023477,002365: 25,2642  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023478,002366: 25,2642           02646 52067                     2CADR    DODES

023482,002370:

Page 549 

023484,002372:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023485,002373: 
023486,002374:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023487,002375:                                                                                                  #  DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023488,002376:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS. INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023489,002377:                                                                                                  #  THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023490,002378:                                                                                                  #  NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY. THE
023491,002379:                                                                                                  #  SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023492,002380:                                                                                                  #  + SHAFT = LOS  . (COS(S), 0, -SIN (S)) (DOT PRODUCT)
023493,002381:                                                                                                  #  -TRUNNION = LOS  . (SIN (T) SIN (S), COS (T), SIN (T) COS (S) )
023494,002382:                                                                                                  #  THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023495,002383:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE
023496,002384:                                                                                                  #  POLARITY OF THE COMMAND. AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023497,002385:                                                                                                  #  SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023498,002386:                                                                                                  #  .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE
023499,002387:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023500,002388:                                                                                                  #  THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023501,002389:                                                                                                  #  CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023502,002390:                                                                                                  #  IS IN PROGRESS. IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023503,002391:                                                                                                  #  OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED. IF NO
023504,002392:                                                                                                  #  CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023505,002393:                                                                                                  #  INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023506,002394:                                                                                                  #  CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023507,002395:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023508,002396:                                                                                                  #  DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023509,002397:                                                                                                  #  (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023510,002398:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023511,002399:                                                                                                  #  PROGRESS. IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023512,002400:                                                                                                  #  LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED. IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023513,002401:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023514,002402:                                                                                                  #  COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023515,002403:                                                                                                  #  CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023516,002404:                                                                                                  #  BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023517,002405:                                                                                                  #  RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL. IF RR DATA GOOD
023518,002406:                                                                                                  #  PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023519,002407:                                                                                                  #  THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023520,002408:                                                                                                  #  AND ENDOFJOB CALLED. IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023521,002409:                                                                                                  #  IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023522,002410:                                                                                                  #  (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023523,002411:                                                                                                  #  VIA ENDOFJOB.
023524,002412: 
023525,002413:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023526,002414:                                                                                                  #  EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023527,002415: 
023528,002416:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023529,002417:                                                                                                  #  RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023530,002418:                                                                                                  #  LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023531,002419: 
023532,002420:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023533,002421:                                                                                                  #  READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
023534,002422:

Page 550 

023536,002424: 
023537,002425:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
023538,002426:                                                                                                  #  NONE
023539,002427: 
023540,002428:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023541,002429: 
023542,002430:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023543,002431: 
023544,002432: 25,2646           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023545,002433: 25,2647           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023546,002434: 25,2650           53107                           DXCH     TANG                                  
023547,002435: 
023548,002436: 25,2651           06042                           TC       INTPRET                               
023549,002437: 
023550,002438: 25,2652           77201                           SETPD    VLOAD                                 
023551,002439: 25,2653           00001                                    0                                     
023552,002440: 25,2654           01101                                    RRTARGET

023599,002487:                                                                                                  #           AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE. CONVERT THIS TO A
023600,002488:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

023607,002495: 25,2732           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023608,002496: 25,2733           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT

024214,003102:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024215,003103:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.  2      BY  J.D. COYNE    SDC    DATE 12-7-66
024216,003104: 
024217,003105:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
024218,003106:                                                                                                  #  1) EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024219,003107:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024220,003108:                                                                                                  #  3) COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024221,003109: 
024222,003110: 
024223,003111:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE       CALL
024224,003112:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
024225,003113: 
024226,003114: 
024227,003115:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
024228,003116: 
024229,003117:                                                                                                  #  LEMPREC,CSMPREC
024230,003118: 
024231,003119:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_ RETURN TO CALLER + 2
024232,003120: 
024233,003121: 
024234,003122:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_ NONE
024235,003123: 
024236,003124: 
024237,003125:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_ NONE
024238,003126: 
024239,003127:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
024240,003128: 
024241,003129:                                                                                                  #  LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
024242,003130:                                                                                                  #  MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV

024367,003255:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024368,003256:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1       BY:  P. VOLANTE  SDC           DATE:  11-15-66
024369,003257: 
024370,003258: 
024371,003259:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024372,003260: 
024373,003261:                                                                                                  #  1) READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE,TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES,THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME. CONVERTS THIS
024374,003262:                                                                                                  #  DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3). CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE,FOR
024375,003263:                                                                                                  #  RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024376,003264: 
024377,003265:                                                                                                  #  2) COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024378,003266: 
024379,003267: 
024380,003268:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024381,003269: 
024382,003270: 
024383,003271:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024384,003272: 
024385,003273:                                                                                                  #         RRRDOT   LPS20.1
024386,003274:                                                                                                  #         RRRANGE  BANKCALL
024387,003275:                                                                                                  #         RADSTALL CDULOGIC
024388,003276:                                                                                                  #         RRNB     SMNB
024389,003277:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT: RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024390,003278: 
024391,003279: 
024392,003280:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024393,003281: 
024394,003282:                                                                                                  #                00001-ERROR EXIT 1-RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024395,003283:                                                                                                  #                00002-ERROR EXIT 2-RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024396,003284: 
024397,003285: 
024398,003286:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521-COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024399,003287:                                                                                                  #   (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024400,003288: 
024401,003289:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT: RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2)-A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024402,003290:                                                                                                  #          RM- THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024403,003291: 
024404,003292:                                                                                                  #     ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024405,003293: 
024406,003294:                                                                                                  #          RDOTM- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING,DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024407,003295:                                                                                                  #          RRTRUN-RR TRUNION ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
024408,003296:                                                                                                  #          RRSHAFT-RR SHAFT ANGLE,DP,IN REVOLUTIONS,SCALED B0
024409,003297:                                                                                                  #          AIG,AMG,AOG-THE CDU ANGLES,THREE SP WORDS
024410,003298:                                                                                                  #          MKTIME-THE TIME OF THE RR READING,DP,IN CENTISECONDS
024411,003299: 
024412,003300: 
024413,003301:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024414,003302: 
024415,003303:                                                                                                  #     RNRAD,THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:
024416,003304:

Page 573

024419,003307:                                                                                                  #      2) RR RANGE RATE,SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024420,003308:

024559,003447:

024561,003449:                                                                                                  #     2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E. THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS
024562,003450: 
024563,003451: 
024564,003452:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE- BANKCALL FOR LRS22.2
024565,003453:

024568,003456:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT - RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO +0 (VIA SWRETURN)
024569,003457:

Page 578 

024615,003503:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME - LSR22.3                                                  DATE - 29 MAY 1967
024616,003504:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                                               LOG SECTION - P20-25
024617,003505:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY - DANFORTH                                                      ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024618,003506: 
024619,003507:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024620,003508: 
024621,003509:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024622,003510:                                                                                                  #  RADAR.(RANGE,RANGE RATE,SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES). THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024623,003511:                                                                                                  #  WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024624,003512: 
024625,003513:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024626,003514:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER O NLY. THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024627,003515:                                                                                                  #  R22LEM  ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM  FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA. IF THE
024628,003516:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED. THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM  TO DISPLAY
024629,003517:                                                                                                  #  THE DEVIATIONS. IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM  RETURNS TO    LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024630,003518:                                                                                                  #  DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR. IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024631,003519:                                                                                                  #  PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK,I.E.,R22LEM  GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024632,003520: 
024633,003521: 
024634,003522:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024635,003523:                                                                                                  #   WLINIT     LGCUPDTE     INTEGRV     INCORP1     ARCTAN
024636,003524:                                                                                                  #   GETULC     RARARANG     INCORP2     NBSM        INTSTALL
024637,003525: 
024638,003526:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024639,003527:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024640,003528:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024641,003529:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024642,003530:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024643,003531:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
024644,003532: 
024645,003533: 
024646,003534:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024647,003535:                                                                                                  #   LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024648,003536:                                                                                                  #   W-MATRIX
024649,003537:                                                                                                  #   MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024650,003538:                                                                                                  #   RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024651,003539:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024652,003540:                                                                                                  #         SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS.B0
024653,003541:                                                                                                  #         TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024654,003542:                                                                                                  #   GIMBAL ANGLES  INNER IN AIG
024655,003543:                                                                                                  #                  MIDDLE IN AMG
024656,003544:                                                                                                  #                  OUTER IN AOG
024657,003545:                                                                                                  #   REFSMMAT
024658,003546:                                                                                                  #   RENDWFLG
024659,003547:                                                                                                  #   NOANGFLG
024660,003548:                                                                                                  #   VEHUPFLG
024661,003549: 
024662,003550:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024663,003551:                                                                                                  #   PUSHLIST--ALL
024664,003552:                                                                                                  #   MX, MY, MZ  (VECTORS)
024665,003553:

Page 579 

024667,003555:                                                                                                  #   ULC,RXZ,SINTHETA,LGRET,RDRET,BVECTOR,W.IND,X78T
024668,003556: 
024669,003557: 
024670,003558: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

025064,003952:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025065,003953:                                                                                                  #  LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025066,003954:                                                                                                  #  COMPUTER ONLY. THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025067,003955:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025068,003956: 
025069,003957:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025070,003958:                                                                                                  #   INSTALL   LGCUPDTE  INCORP1   RP-TO-R
025071,003959:                                                                                                  #   INTEGRV   GETULC    INCORP2
025072,003960: 
025073,003961:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025074,003962:                                                                                                  #   CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025075,003963:                                                                                                  #   NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025076,003964:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025077,003965:                                                                                                  #   MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025078,003966:                                                                                                  #   UPDATED W-MATRIX
025079,003967:

Page 587

025086,003974:                                                                                                  #         RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7

025228,004116: 
025229,004117:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTES SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
025230,004118:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC
025231,004119:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025232,004120:                                                                                                  #   ULC IN ULC, PD0
025233,004121:                                                                                                  #   RLC IN PD36D
025234,004122:                                                                                                  #   SIN THETA IN SINTHETA AND PD6
025235,004123:                                                                                                  #   RXZ NORM IN RXZ (N IN X1)

025288,004176: 
025289,004177:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1   RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025290,004178:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO  0        BY  P VOLANTE   SDC         DATE 1-15-67
025291,004179: 
025292,004180: 
025293,004181:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025294,004182: 
025295,004183:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025296,004184:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025297,004185:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS. IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025298,004186:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025299,004187: 
025300,004188: 
025301,004189:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025302,004190: 
025303,004191: 
025304,004192:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025305,004193: 
025306,004194:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC      R61LEM
025307,004195:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC      RRDESSM
025308,004196:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY      FLAGDOWN
025309,004197:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST      FLAGUP
025310,004198:                                                                                                  #        RRNB          BANKCALL
025311,004199: 
025312,004200: 
025313,004201:                                                                                                  #  EXIT  - TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025314,004202: 
025315,004203: 
025316,004204:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025317,004205: 
025318,004206:                                                                                                  #      DATAGOOD (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R1- 00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025319,004207:                                                                                                  #                                       11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025320,004208:                                                                                                  #      OMEGAD   (SP)-FOR DISPLAY IN R2- ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGHT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025321,004209: 
025322,004210:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
025323,004211:                                                                                                  #     SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025324,004212:                                                                                                  #     LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025325,004213:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025326,004214: 
025327,004215:                                                                                                  #     RLMSRCH      UXVECT
025328,004216:                                                                                                  #     VXRLM        UYVECT
025329,004217:                                                                                                  #     LOSDESRD     NSRCHPNT
025330,004218:                                                                                                  #     DATAGOOD     OMEGAD
025331,004219:                                                                                                  #     MPAC         PUSHLIST
025332,004220: 
025333,004221: 
025334,004222: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025335,004223: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO

025337,004225: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025338,004226: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND

Page 592

025551,004439:    6030  E7,1471                                  EBANK=   WHOCARES                              
025552,004440:    6030           03041 66107  VB56CADR           2CADR    TRMTRACK

025555,004443:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29  (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025556,004444:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2       BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025557,004445: 
025558,004446: 
025559,004447:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025560,004448: 
025561,004449:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025562,004450:                                                                                                  #  AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025563,004451:                                                                                                  #  THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025564,004452:                                                                                                  #  THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025565,004453:                                                                                                  #  DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025566,004454:                                                                                                  #  INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025567,004455: 
025568,004456:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025569,004457: 
025570,004458: 
025571,004459:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025572,004460: 
025573,004461:                                                                                                  #  REMODE   RRTONLY
025574,004462:                                                                                                  #  UNIT     MPACVBUF
025575,004463:                                                                                                  #  QUICTRIG AX*SR*T
025576,004464:                                                                                                  #  SPSIN    SPCOS
025577,004465:                                                                                                  #  SETRRECR RROUT
025578,004466:                                                                                                  #  RRRDOT   RRRANGE
025579,004467: 
025580,004468: 
025581,004469:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025582,004470: 
025583,004471: 
025584,004472:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025585,004473: 
025586,004474:                                                                                                  #  RM       RDOTM                  (RAW)
025587,004475:                                                                                                  #  AIG      AMG
025588,004476:                                                                                                  #  AOG      TRKMKCNT               TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025589,004477:                                                                                                  #  TANGNB   TANGNB +1              OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025590,004478:                                                                                                  #  MKTIME
025591,004479:

Page 598 

025593,004481: 
025594,004482:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025595,004483: 
025596,004484:                                                                                                  #  NOR29FLG READRFLG               (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START)  (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025597,004485:                                                                                                  #  PIPTIME  RADMODES (BIT 10)      (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025598,004486:                                                                                                  #  R(CSM)   V(CSM)
025599,004487:                                                                                                  #  R        V                      (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025600,004488: 
025601,004489: 
025602,004490:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025603,004491: 
025604,004492:                                                                                                  #  RADMODES (BIT 10)
025605,004493:                                                                                                  #  LOSSM    LOSVDT/4       (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025606,004494:                                                                                                  #  SAVECDUT OLDESFLG       (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025607,004495:                                                                                                  #  LOSCMFLG READRFLG
025608,004496: 
025609,004497: 
025610,004498:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025611,004499: 
025612,004500: 
025613,004501:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025614,004502: 
025615,004503:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE;  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025616,004504:                                                                                                  #  DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025617,004505:                                                                                                  #  RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.

025797,004685:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025798,004686: 
025799,004687:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025800,004688:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025801,004689:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025802,004690:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025803,004691:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025804,004692: 
025805,004693:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025806,004694:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025807,004695: 
025808,004696: 
025809,004697: 32,2550                                           BANK     32                                    
025810,004698: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025811,004699: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025812,004700: 
025813,004701: 32,2550                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025814,004702: 32,2550  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025815,004703: 
025816,004704: 32,2550           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025817,004705: 32,2551           55106                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025818,004706: 32,2552           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025819,004707: 
025820,004708: 32,2553           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025821,004709: 32,2554           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025822,004710: 32,2555           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025823,004711: 32,2556           12564                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025824,004712: 
025825,004713: 32,2557           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025826,004714: 32,2560           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025827,004715: 32,2561           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025828,004716: 32,2562           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025829,004717: 32,2563           21101                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025830,004718: 
025831,004719: 32,2564           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025832,004720: 32,2565           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025833,004721: 32,2566           31101                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025834,004722: 32,2567           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025835,004723: 32,2570           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025836,004724: 32,2571           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025837,004725: 32,2572           12600                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025838,004726: 
025839,004727: 32,2573           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025840,004728: 32,2574           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025841,004729: 32,2575           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025842,004730: 32,2576           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025843,004731: 32,2577           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025844,004732: 
025845,004733: 32,2600           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025846,004734: 32,2601           12553                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025847,004735:

Page 604 

025849,004737:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025850,004738: 
025851,004739: 32,2602           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
025852,004740: 32,2603           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
025853,004741: 32,2604           32775                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15 + -34D
025854,004742: 32,2605           54120                           TS       FIXLOC                                
025855,004743: 32,2606           04713                           TC       USPRCADR                              #  WITH FIXLOC ARMED FOR LENGTH AND LENGTH
025856,004744: 32,2607           01023                           CADR     UNIT                                  #  SQUARED, BORROW UNITIZING ROUTINE.
025857,004745: 32,2610           07535                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
025858,004746: 
025859,004747: 32,2611           11106                           CCS      TANG                                  
025860,004748: 32,2612           12614                           TCF      +2                                    
025861,004749: 32,2613           12630                           TCF      GOTANGLS                              #  GET CDU ANGLES ONLY AFTER 1ST PASS.
025862,004750: 32,2614           00004                           INHINT                                         #  ENSURE CONSISTENT CDU READINGS.
